<h1><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Overview</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-about-c4" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#about-c4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>About C4</h2>
<p>Code 432n4 (C4) is an open organization consisting of security researchers, auditors, developers, and individuals with domain expertise in smart contracts.</p>
<p>A C4 code contest is an event in which community participants, referred to as Wardens, review, audit, or analyze smart contract logic in exchange for a bounty provided by sponsoring projects.</p>
<p>During the code contest outlined in this document, C4 conducted an analysis of the Sushi Miso contest smart contract system written in Solidity. The code contest took place between September 9—September 15 2021.</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-wardens" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#wardens"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Wardens</h2>
<p>11 Wardens contributed reports to the Sushi Miso contest code contest:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/WatchPug_" rel="nofollow">WatchPug</a></li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/0xRajeev" rel="nofollow">0xRajeev</a></li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/cmichelio" rel="nofollow">cmichel</a></li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/gpersoon" rel="nofollow">gpersoon</a></li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/MukeshJ_eth" rel="nofollow">JMukesh</a></li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/liam_eastwood13" rel="nofollow">leastwood</a></li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/_hrkrshnn" rel="nofollow">hrkrshnn</a></li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/SolidityDev" rel="nofollow">pauliax</a></li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/itsmeSTYJ" rel="nofollow">itsmeSTYJ</a></li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/loop_225" rel="nofollow">loop</a></li>
</ul>
<p>This contest was judged by <a href="https://twitter.com/ghoulsol" rel="nofollow">ghoul.sol</a>.</p>
<p>Final report assembled by <a href="https://twitter.com/itsmetechjay" rel="nofollow">itsmetechjay</a> and <a href="https://twitter.com/CloudEllie1" rel="nofollow">CloudEllie</a>.</p>
<h1><a id="user-content-summary" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#summary"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Summary</h1>
<p>The C4 analysis yielded an aggregated total of 101 unique vulnerabilities. All of the issues presented here are linked back to their original finding.</p>
<p>Of these vulnerabilities, 3 received a risk rating in the category of HIGH severity, 1 received a risk rating in the category of MEDIUM severity, and 21 received a risk rating in the category of LOW severity.</p>
<p>C4 analysis also identified 47 non-critical recommendations and 29 gas optimizations.</p>
<h1><a id="user-content-scope" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#scope"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Scope</h1>
<p>The code under review can be found within the <a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso">C4 Sushi Miso contest repository</a> and is composed of 106 smart contracts written in the Solidity programming language, and includes 4,040 lines of Solidity code.</p>
<h1><a id="user-content-severity-criteria" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#severity-criteria"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Severity Criteria</h1>
<p>C4 assesses the severity of disclosed vulnerabilities according to a methodology based on <a href="https://owasp.org/www-community/OWASP_Risk_Rating_Methodology" rel="nofollow">OWASP standards</a>.</p>
<p>Vulnerabilities are divided into three primary risk categories: high, medium, and low.</p>
<p>High-level considerations for vulnerabilities span the following key areas when conducting assessments:</p>
<ul>
<li>Malicious Input Handling</li>
<li>Escalation of privileges</li>
<li>Arithmetic</li>
<li>Gas use</li>
</ul>
<p>Further information regarding the severity criteria referenced throughout the submission review process, please refer to the documentation provided on <a href="https://code423n4.com" rel="nofollow">the C4 website</a>.</p>
<h1><a id="user-content-high-risk-findings-3" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#high-risk-findings-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>High Risk Findings (3)</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-h-01-postauctionlaunchersolfinalize-adding-liquidity-to-an-existing-pool-may-allows-the-attacker-to-steal-most-of-the-tokens" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#h-01-postauctionlaunchersolfinalize-adding-liquidity-to-an-existing-pool-may-allows-the-attacker-to-steal-most-of-the-tokens"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/14">[H-01] <code>PostAuctionLauncher.sol#finalize()</code> Adding liquidity to an existing pool may allows the attacker to steal most of the tokens</a></h2>
<p><em>Submitted by WatchPug, also found by 0xRajeev and cmichel.</em></p>
<p><code>PostAuctionLauncher.finalize()</code> can be called by anyone, and it sends tokens directly to the pair pool to mint liquidity, even when the pair pool exists.</p>
<p>An attacker may control the LP price by creating the pool and then call <code>finalize()</code> to mint LP token with unfair price (pay huge amounts of tokens and get few amounts of LP token), and then remove the initial liquidity they acquired when creating the pool and take out huge amounts of tokens.</p>
<p><a href="https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/blob/2cdb1486a55ded55c81898b7be8811cb68cfda9e/contracts/Liquidity/PostAuctionLauncher.sol#L257">https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/blob/2cdb1486a55ded55c81898b7be8811cb68cfda9e/contracts/Liquidity/PostAuctionLauncher.sol#L257</a></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/**
 * @notice Finalizes Token sale and launches LP.
 * @return liquidity Number of LPs.
 */
function finalize() external nonReentrant returns (uint256 liquidity) {
    // GP: Can we remove admin, let anyone can finalise and launch?
    // require(hasAdminRole(msg.sender) || hasOperatorRole(msg.sender), &quot;PostAuction: Sender must be operator&quot;);
    require(marketConnected(), &quot;PostAuction: Auction must have this launcher address set as the destination wallet&quot;);
    require(!launcherInfo.launched);

    if (!market.finalized()) {
        market.finalize();
    }
    require(market.finalized());

    launcherInfo.launched = true;
    if (!market.auctionSuccessful() ) {
        return 0;
    }

    /// @dev if the auction is settled in weth, wrap any contract balance 
    uint256 launcherBalance = address(this).balance;
    if (launcherBalance &gt; 0 ) {
        IWETH(weth).deposit{value : launcherBalance}();
    }
    
    (uint256 token1Amount, uint256 token2Amount) =  getTokenAmounts();

    /// @dev cannot start a liquidity pool with no tokens on either side
    if (token1Amount == 0 || token2Amount == 0 ) {
        return 0;
    }

    address pair = factory.getPair(address(token1), address(token2));
    if(pair == address(0)) {
        createPool();
    }

    /// @dev add liquidity to pool via the pair directly
    _safeTransfer(address(token1), tokenPair, token1Amount);
    _safeTransfer(address(token2), tokenPair, token2Amount);
    liquidity = IUniswapV2Pair(tokenPair).mint(address(this));
    launcherInfo.liquidityAdded = BoringMath.to128(uint256(launcherInfo.liquidityAdded).add(liquidity));

    /// @dev if unlock time not yet set, add it.
    if (launcherInfo.unlock == 0 ) {
        launcherInfo.unlock = BoringMath.to64(block.timestamp + uint256(launcherInfo.locktime));
    }
    emit LiquidityAdded(liquidity);
}
"><pre lang="solidity=216"><code>/**
 * @notice Finalizes Token sale and launches LP.
 * @return liquidity Number of LPs.
 */
function finalize() external nonReentrant returns (uint256 liquidity) {
    // GP: Can we remove admin, let anyone can finalise and launch?
    // require(hasAdminRole(msg.sender) || hasOperatorRole(msg.sender), "PostAuction: Sender must be operator");
    require(marketConnected(), "PostAuction: Auction must have this launcher address set as the destination wallet");
    require(!launcherInfo.launched);

    if (!market.finalized()) {
        market.finalize();
    }
    require(market.finalized());

    launcherInfo.launched = true;
    if (!market.auctionSuccessful() ) {
        return 0;
    }

    /// @dev if the auction is settled in weth, wrap any contract balance 
    uint256 launcherBalance = address(this).balance;
    if (launcherBalance &gt; 0 ) {
        IWETH(weth).deposit{value : launcherBalance}();
    }
    
    (uint256 token1Amount, uint256 token2Amount) =  getTokenAmounts();

    /// @dev cannot start a liquidity pool with no tokens on either side
    if (token1Amount == 0 || token2Amount == 0 ) {
        return 0;
    }

    address pair = factory.getPair(address(token1), address(token2));
    if(pair == address(0)) {
        createPool();
    }

    /// @dev add liquidity to pool via the pair directly
    _safeTransfer(address(token1), tokenPair, token1Amount);
    _safeTransfer(address(token2), tokenPair, token2Amount);
    liquidity = IUniswapV2Pair(tokenPair).mint(address(this));
    launcherInfo.liquidityAdded = BoringMath.to128(uint256(launcherInfo.liquidityAdded).add(liquidity));

    /// @dev if unlock time not yet set, add it.
    if (launcherInfo.unlock == 0 ) {
        launcherInfo.unlock = BoringMath.to64(block.timestamp + uint256(launcherInfo.locktime));
    }
    emit LiquidityAdded(liquidity);
}
</code></pre></div>
<p>In line 257, <code>PostAuctionLauncher</code> will mint LP with <code>token1Amount</code> and <code>token2Amount</code>. The amounts (<code>token1Amount</code> and <code>token2Amount</code>) are computed according to the auction result, without considering the current price (reserves) of the existing <code>tokenPair</code>.</p>
<p>See <a href="https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/blob/2cdb1486a55ded55c81898b7be8811cb68cfda9e/contracts/Liquidity/PostAuctionLauncher.sol#L268">PostAuctionLauncher.getTokenAmounts()</a></p>
<p><code>PostAuctionLauncher</code> will receive an unfairly low amount of lp token because the amounts sent to <code>tokenPair</code> didn't match the current price of the pair.</p>
<p>See <a href="https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/blob/2cdb1486a55ded55c81898b7be8811cb68cfda9e/contracts/UniswapV2/UniswapV2Pair.sol#L135">UniswapV2Pair.mint(...)</a></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="liquidity = MathUniswap.min(amount0.mul(_totalSupply) / _reserve0, amount1.mul(_totalSupply) / _reserve1);
"><pre lang="solidity=135"><code>liquidity = MathUniswap.min(amount0.mul(_totalSupply) / _reserve0, amount1.mul(_totalSupply) / _reserve1);
</code></pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-impact" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#impact"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Impact</h4>
<p>Lose a majority share of the tokens.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-proof-of-concept" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#proof-of-concept"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Proof of Concept</h4>
<ol>
<li>The attacker creates LP with 0.0000001 token1 and 1000 token2, receives 0.01 LP token;</li>
<li>Call <code>PostAuctionLauncher.finalize()</code>. PostAuctionLauncher will mint liquidity with 2000 token1 and 1000 token2 for example, receives only  0.01 LP token;</li>
<li>The attacker removes all his LP, receives 1000 token1 (most of which come from <code>PostAuctionLauncher</code>).</li>
</ol>
<h4><a id="user-content-recommended-mitigation-steps" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#recommended-mitigation-steps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Recommended Mitigation Steps</h4>
<p>To only support tokenPair created by <code>PostAuctionLauncher</code> or check for the token price before mint liquidity.</p>
<p><strong><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/14#issuecomment-934641852">Clearwood (Sushi Miso) confirmed and patched</a>:</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p><a href="https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/pull/21">https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/pull/21</a></p>
</blockquote>
<h2><a id="user-content-h-02-sushitoken-transfers-are-broken-due-to-wrong-delegates-accounting-on-transfers" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#h-02-sushitoken-transfers-are-broken-due-to-wrong-delegates-accounting-on-transfers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/117">[H-02] SushiToken transfers are broken due to wrong delegates accounting on transfers</a></h2>
<p><em>Submitted by cmichel</em>.</p>
<p>When minting / transferring / burning tokens, the <code>SushiToken._beforeTokenTransfer</code> function is called and supposed to correctly shift the voting power due to the increase/decrease in tokens for the <code>from</code> and <code>to</code> accounts.
However, it does not correctly do that, it tries to shift the votes from the <code>from</code> account, instead of the <strong><code>_delegates[from]</code></strong> account.
This can lead to transfers reverting.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-proof-of-concept-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#proof-of-concept-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Proof Of Concept</h4>
<p>Imagine the following transactions on the <code>SushiToken</code> contract.
We'll illustrate the corresponding <code>_moveDelegates</code> calls and written checkpoints for each.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>mint(A, 1000) = transfer(0, A, 1000)</code> =&gt; <code>_moveDelegates(0, delegates[A]=0) </code> =&gt; no checkpoints are written to anyone because delegatees are still zero</li>
<li>A delegates to A' =&gt; <code>_moveDelegates(0, A')</code> =&gt; <code>writeCheckpoint(A', 1000)</code></li>
<li>B delegates to B' =&gt; no checkpoints are written as B has a zero balance</li>
<li><code>transfer(A, B, 1000)</code> =&gt; <code>_moveDelegates(A, delegates[B] = B')</code> =&gt; underflows when subtracting <code>amount=1000</code> from A's non-existent checkpoint (defaults to 0 votes)</li>
</ul>
<p>It should subtract from A's delegatee <code>A'</code>'s checkpoint instead.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-impact-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#impact-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Impact</h4>
<p>Users that delegated votes will be unable to transfer any of their tokens.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-recommended-mitigation-steps-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#recommended-mitigation-steps-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Recommended Mitigation Steps</h4>
<p>In <code>SushiToken._beforeTokenTransfer</code>, change the <code>_moveDelegates</code> call to be from <code>_delegates[from]</code> instead:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="function _beforeTokenTransfer(address from, address to, uint256 amount) internal override { 
    _moveDelegates(_delegates[from], _delegates[to], amount);
    super._beforeTokenTransfer(from, to, amount);
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">function<span class="pl-en"> _beforeTokenTransfer</span></span>(<span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">from</span>, <span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">to</span>, <span class="pl-c1">uint256</span> <span class="pl-v">amount</span>) <span class="pl-k">internal</span> <span class="pl-k">override</span> { 
    <span class="pl-c1">_moveDelegates</span>(_delegates[from], _delegates[to], amount);
    super.<span class="pl-c1">_beforeTokenTransfer</span>(from, to, amount);
}</pre></div>
<p>This is also how the <a href="https://github.com/compound-finance/compound-protocol/blob/master/contracts/Governance/Comp.sol#L241">original code from Compound</a> does it.</p>
<p><strong><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/117#issuecomment-920570459">maxsam4 (Sushi Miso) acknowledged</a>:</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>This is a known issue in Sushi token but was kept unchanged in MISO for "preservation of history :)". That was not necessarily a wise choice lol. I think 1 severity should be fine for this as this was an intentional thing. The delegate feature is not supposed to be used in these tokens. We might create a new token type with this bug fixed.</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/117#issuecomment-934637612">ghoul-sol (judge) commented</a>:</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>We have crazy wallets on the blockchain that will call every possible function available to them and that's why I'm keeping this as is. Even intentional, the issue stands so the warden should get credit for it.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2><a id="user-content-h-03-last-person-to-withdraw-his-tokens-might-not-be-able-to-do-this-in-crowdsale-edge-case" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#h-03-last-person-to-withdraw-his-tokens-might-not-be-able-to-do-this-in-crowdsale-edge-case"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/15">[H-03] Last person to withdraw his tokens might not be able to do this, in Crowdsale (edge case)</a></h2>
<p><em>Submitted by gpersoon</em>.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-impact-2" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#impact-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Impact</h4>
<p>Suppose a Crowdsale is successful and enough commitments are made before the <code>marketInfo.endTime</code>.
Suppose marketStatus.commitmentsTotal  == marketInfo.totalTokens -1      // note this is an edge case, but can be constructed by an attacker
Then the function <code>auctionEnded()</code> returns true
Assume <code>auctionSuccessful()</code> is also true (might depend on the config of <code>marketPrice.goal</code> and <code>marketInfo.totalTokens</code>)
Then an admin can call <code>finalize()</code> to finalize the Crowdsale.
The function finalize distributes the funds and the unsold tokens and sets <code>status.finalized = true</code> so that finalized cannot be called again.
Now we have "marketInfo.totalTokens -1" tokens left in the contract</p>
<p>However <code>commitEth()</code> or <code>commitTokens()</code> can still be called (they give no error message that the auction has ended)
Then functions call <code>calculateCommitment</code>, which luckily prevent from buying too much, however 1 token can still be bought
These functions also call <code>\_addCommitment()</code>, which only checks for <code>marketInfo.endTime</code>, which hasn't passed yet.</p>
<p>Now an extra token is sold and the contract has 1 token short. So the last person to withdraw his tokens cannot withdraw them (because you cannot specify how much you want to withdraw)</p>
<p>Also the revenues for the last token cannot be retrieved as <code>finalize()</code> cannot be called again.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-proof-of-concept-2" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#proof-of-concept-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Proof of Concept</h4>
<p><a href="https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/blob/master/contracts/Auctions/Crowdsale.sol#L374">https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/blob/master/contracts/Auctions/Crowdsale.sol#L374</a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" function finalize() public nonReentrant {
        require(hasAdminRole(msg.sender) || wallet == msg.sender || hasSmartContractRole(msg.sender) || finalizeTimeExpired(),&quot;Crowdsale: sender must be an admin&quot;); // can be called by admin
        MarketStatus storage status = marketStatus;
        require(!status.finalized, &quot;Crowdsale: already finalized&quot;);
        MarketInfo storage info = marketInfo;
        require(auctionEnded(), &quot;Crowdsale: Has not finished yet&quot;);    // is true if enough sold, even if this is before marketInfo.endTime

        if (auctionSuccessful()) {          
            /// @dev Transfer contributed tokens to wallet.
            /// @dev Transfer unsold tokens to wallet.
        } else {
            /// @dev Return auction tokens back to wallet.
        }
        status.finalized = true;

function auctionEnded() public view returns (bool) {
        return block.timestamp &gt; uint256(marketInfo.endTime) || 
        _getTokenAmount(uint256(marketStatus.commitmentsTotal) + 1) &gt;= uint256(marketInfo.totalTokens); // is true if enough sold, even if this is before marketInfo.endTime
    }

function auctionSuccessful() public view returns (bool) {
        return uint256(marketStatus.commitmentsTotal) &gt;= uint256(marketPrice.goal);
}

function commitEth(address payable _beneficiary, bool readAndAgreedToMarketParticipationAgreement ) public payable nonReentrant  {
       ...
        uint256 ethToTransfer = calculateCommitment(msg.value);
       ...
       _addCommitment(_beneficiary, ethToTransfer);
   
 function calculateCommitment(uint256 _commitment) public view returns (uint256 committed) { // this prevents buying too much
        uint256 tokens = _getTokenAmount(_commitment);
        uint256 tokensCommited =_getTokenAmount(uint256(marketStatus.commitmentsTotal));
        if ( tokensCommited.add(tokens) &gt; uint256(marketInfo.totalTokens)) {
            return _getTokenPrice(uint256(marketInfo.totalTokens).sub(tokensCommited));
        }
        return _commitment;
    }

function _addCommitment(address _addr, uint256 _commitment) internal {
        require(block.timestamp &gt;= uint256(marketInfo.startTime) &amp;&amp; block.timestamp &lt;= uint256(marketInfo.endTime), &quot;Crowdsale: outside auction hours&quot;); // doesn't check auctionEnded() nor status.finalized
        ...
        uint256 newCommitment = commitments[_addr].add(_commitment);
        ...
        commitments[_addr] = newCommitment;

function withdrawTokens(address payable beneficiary) public   nonReentrant  {    
        if (auctionSuccessful()) {
            ...
            uint256 tokensToClaim = tokensClaimable(beneficiary);
            ...
            claimed[beneficiary] = claimed[beneficiary].add(tokensToClaim);
            _safeTokenPayment(auctionToken, beneficiary, tokensToClaim);    // will fail is last token is missing
        } else {



## Tools Used

## Recommended Mitigation Steps
In the function _addCommitment, add a check on auctionEnded() or status.finalized

## <span class="pl-v">Tools</span> <span class="pl-v">Used</span>

## <span class="pl-v">Recommended</span> <span class="pl-v">Mitigation</span> <span class="pl-v">Steps</span>
<span class="pl-v">In</span> <span class="pl-s1">the</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-s1">_addCommitment</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">add</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-s1">check</span> <span class="pl-s1">on</span> <span class="pl-s1">auctionEnded</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-s1">or</span> <span class="pl-s1">status</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-s1">finalized</span></pre></div>
<p><strong><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/15#issuecomment-934641167">Clearwood (Sushi Miso) confirmed and patched</a>:</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p><a href="https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/pull/20">https://github.com/sushiswap/miso/pull/20</a></p>
</blockquote>
<h1><a id="user-content-medium-risk-findings-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#medium-risk-findings-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Medium Risk Findings (1)</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-m-01-use-of-transfer-instead-of-call--to-send-eth" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#m-01-use-of-transfer-instead-of-call--to-send-eth"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/87">[M-01] use of transfer() instead of call()  to send eth</a></h2>
<p><em>Submitted by JMukesh</em>.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-impact-3" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#impact-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Impact</h4>
<p>Use of <code>transfer()</code> might render ETH impossible to withdraw because after istanbul hardfork, there is an increase in the gas cost of the SLOAD operation and therefore breaks some existing smart contracts.Those contracts will break because their fallback functions used to consume less than 2300 gas, and they’ll now consume more, since 2300 the amount of gas a contract’s fallback function receives if it’s called via Solidity’s <code>transfer()</code> or <code>send()</code> methods.
Any smart contract that uses <code>transfer()</code> or <code>send()</code> is taking a hard dependency on gas costs by forwarding a fixed amount of gas: 2300.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="https://consensys.net/diligence/blog/2019/09/stop-using-soliditys-transfer-now/" rel="nofollow">https://consensys.net/diligence/blog/2019/09/stop-using-soliditys-transfer-now/</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><a href="https://blog.openzeppelin.com/opyn-gamma-protocol-audit/" rel="nofollow">https://blog.openzeppelin.com/opyn-gamma-protocol-audit/</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-proof-of-concept-3" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#proof-of-concept-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Proof of Concept</h4>

<h4><a id="user-content-tools-used" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tools-used"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Tools Used</h4>
<p>manual review</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-recommended-mitigation-steps-2" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#recommended-mitigation-steps-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Recommended Mitigation Steps</h4>
<p>use <code>call()</code> to send eth</p>
<p><strong><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/87#issuecomment-920589153">maxsam4 (Sushi Miso) disputed and commented</a>:</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>This is intentional, not a risk. The contract does not want to give any gas stipend to the destination.</p>
<p>Even if the user messes up, <code>misoDev</code> address can be changed to a proper address later.</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/87#issuecomment-934654221">ghoul-sol (judge) commented</a>:</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>using <code>.transfer</code> can make ETH transfer to a smart contract impossible. User can always change the address however I agree with warden that this is an issue.</p>
</blockquote>

<h1><a id="user-content-gas-optimizations-29" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#gas-optimizations-29"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Gas Optimizations (29)</h1>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/36">[G-01] Slot packing saves slots but increases runtime gas consumption due to masking</a>
<em>Submitted by 0xRajeev</em>.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/42">[G-02] Caching state variables in local/memory variables avoids SLOADs to save gas</a>
<em>Submitted by 0xRajeev</em>.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/60">[G-03] Avoiding initialization of loop index can save a little gas</a>
<em>Submitted by 0xRajeev</em>.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/62">[G-04] Check for zero msg.value can save gas</a>
<em>Submitted by 0xRajeev</em>.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/65">[G-05] Using function parameters in emits saves gas</a>
<em>Submitted by 0xRajeev</em>.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/66">[G-06] Avoiding unnecessary external call will save &gt; 2600 gas</a>
<em>Submitted by 0xRajeev</em>.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/68">[G-07] Unnecessary zero check on variable which is never initialized earlier</a>
<em>Submitted by 0xRajeev</em>.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2021-09-sushimiso-findings/issues/90">[G-08] unused local variable</a>

<h1><a id="user-content-disclosures" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#disclosures"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Disclosures</h1>
<p>C4 is an open organization governed by participants in the community.</p>
<p>C4 Contests incentivize the discovery of exploits, vulnerabilities, and bugs in smart contracts. Security researchers are rewarded at an increasing rate for finding higher-risk issues. Contest submissions are judged by a knowledgeable security researcher and solidity developer and disclosed to sponsoring developers. C4 does not conduct formal verification regarding the provided code but instead provides final verification.</p>
<p>C4 does not provide any guarantee or warranty regarding the security of this project. All smart contract software should be used at the sole risk and responsibility of users.</p>
</article>
